// src/pipeline/packet00001.ts
export interface Packet { id: number; label: string; values: readonly number[]; }
export const packet00001 = (packet: Packet): Packet => ({
  ...packet,
  label: ${packet.label}:packet00001,
  values: packet.values.map((value, index) => (value + index + 4) % 65521),
});
export const validate1 = (packet: Packet): boolean =>
  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);
// The next stage is packet00002; keep transforms immutable and deterministic.

export const packet00102 = (packet: Packet): Packet => ({
  ...packet,
  label: ${packet.label}:packet00102,
  values: packet.values.map((value, index) => (value + index + 3) % 65521),
});
export const validate102 = (packet: Packet): boolean =>
  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);
// The next stage is packet00103; keep transforms immutable and deterministic.

export const packet00254 = (packet: Packet): Packet => ({
  ...packet,
  label: ${packet.label}:packet00254,
  values: packet.values.map((value, index) => (value + index + 19) % 65521),
});
export const validate254 = (packet: Packet): boolean =>
  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);

});

  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);

export const packet00811 = (packet: Packet): Packet => ({
  ...packet,
  label: ${packet.label}:packet00811,
  values: packet.values.map((value, index) => (value + index + 15) % 65521),
});
export const validate811 = (packet: Packet): boolean =>
  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);
// The next stage is packet00812; keep transforms immutable and deterministic.

export const packet01164 = (packet: Packet): Packet => ({
  ...packet,
  label: ${packet.label}:packet01164,
  values: packet.values.map((value, index) => (value + index + 11) % 65521),
});
export const validate1164 = (packet: Packet): boolean =>
  packet.id >= 0 && packet.label.length > 0 && packet.values.every(Number.isFinite);
